Finger assignments:
's' -> finger 1 (row=1, col=1)
'a' -> finger 0 (row=1, col=0)
'p' -> finger 9 (row=0, col=9)
'o' -> finger 8 (row=0, col=8)
'u' -> finger 6 (row=0, col=6)
'y' -> finger 6 (row=0, col=5)
't' -> finger 3 (row=0, col=4)
'r' -> finger 3 (row=0, col=3)
'e' -> finger 2 (row=0, col=2)
'w' -> finger 1 (row=0, col=1)
'd' -> finger 2 (row=1, col=2)
'q' -> finger 0 (row=0, col=0)
'f' -> finger 3 (row=1, col=3)
',' -> finger 7 (row=2, col=7)
'g' -> finger 3 (row=1, col=4)
'h' -> finger 6 (row=1, col=5)
'i' -> finger 7 (row=0, col=7)
'.' -> finger 8 (row=2, col=8)
'/' -> finger 9 (row=2, col=9)
'j' -> finger 6 (row=1, col=6)
'k' -> finger 7 (row=1, col=7)
'l' -> finger 8 (row=1, col=8)
'z' -> finger 0 (row=2, col=0)
'x' -> finger 1 (row=2, col=1)
'c' -> finger 2 (row=2, col=2)
';' -> finger 9 (row=1, col=9)
'v' -> finger 3 (row=2, col=3)
'b' -> finger 3 (row=2, col=4)
'n' -> finger 6 (row=2, col=5)
'm' -> finger 6 (row=2, col=6)
